[What's the SECRET to Jordan The Stallion's 13M TikTok Followers?](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=HNHbv3ghvw8)

•

•

36,406 views1 year ago

In this episode of Creator Spotlight, host Shira Lazar interviews Jordan Howlett (aka @Jordan\_The\_Stallion8) TikTok sensation and president of the Fast Food Secrets Club. Together, they explore the nonlinear journey that took Jordan from Division 1 baseball player to over 13 million followers in TikTok.

Learn the unique way he works with brands as Jordan shares the core philosophies that help him stay productive, ambitious and productive; including the roles that faith, family and fun play in each.

Discover how a commitment to authenticity and bold moves led him to collaborations with Kevin Hart, Donald Glover, Halle Berry and Method Man just to name a few.

## [Posts](https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCJ7LKwgheOe8OHD5YWnlPUg/posts "Posts")  [Posts](https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCJ7LKwgheOe8OHD5YWnlPUg/posts)

🚨 Epic Games has reportedly confirmed that Fortnite players can now receive refunds for all cosmetics tied to the artist D4vd, including popular emotes like "Feel It" and "Trophy Drop."

This decision follows serious criminal charges against the 21-year-old singer, David Anthony Burke, involving the murder of a 14-year-old girl. The community had been calling for the removal of these items for some time, expressing a desire to distance their in-game accounts from the artist's work.⁠
⁠
Currently, players must manually contact Epic Player Support to request their V-Bucks back. However, starting Tuesday, April 28, the company will launch an automated self-service refund option specifically for these items. This update aims to streamline the process for anyone who purchased the emotes or Jam Tracks, such as "What Are You Waiting For" and "Locked and Loaded," making it easier for the player base to return the content immediately.⁠
⁠
Epic Games also signaled that this is only the beginning, stating that a "bunch of changes" will be rolled out over time. While they have not yet confirmed if the items will be permanently scrubbed from the game, many players are pushing for the total removal of these cosmetics from all lockers, including those earned through tournaments. ⁠
⁠
The ongoing rollout suggests that Epic is actively evaluating how to handle the presence of the artist's content within the Fortnite ecosystem moving forward.⁠
⁠
Link in bio to catch up on the artists arrest. ⁠
⁠

🚨 Epic Games has reportedly confirmed that Fortnite players can now receive refunds for all cosmetics tied to the artist D4vd, including popular emotes like "Feel It" and "Trophy Drop."

This decision follows serious criminal charges against the 21-year-old singer, David Anthony Burke, involving the murder of a 14-year-old girl. The community had been calling for the removal of these items for some time, expressing a desire to distance their in-game accounts from the artist's work.⁠
⁠
Currently, players must manually contact Epic Player Support to request their V-Bucks back. However, starting Tuesday, April 28, the company will launch an automated self-service refund option specifically for these items. This update aims to streamline the process for anyone who purchased the emotes or Jam Tracks, such as "What Are You Waiting For" and "Locked and Loaded," making it easier for the player base to return the content immediately.⁠
⁠
Epic Games also signaled that this is only the beginning, stating that a "bunch of changes" will be rolled out over time. While they have not yet confirmed if the items will be permanently scrubbed from the game, many players are pushing for the total removal of these cosmetics from all lockers, including those earned through tournaments. ⁠
⁠
The ongoing rollout suggests that Epic is actively evaluating how to handle the presence of the artist's content within the Fortnite ecosystem moving forward.⁠

Actor Ruby Rose has publicly accused singer Katy Perry of sexual assault, stemming from an incident allegedly occurring nearly two decades ago. ⁠
⁠
Rose shared the allegations via the social media platform Threads, claiming the encounter took place at the Spice Market nightclub in Melbourne when she was in her early 20s. According to Rose, she previously framed the event as a humorous anecdote but has now decided to speak openly about the trauma she experienced.⁠
⁠
Rose provided specific details of the alleged assault, claiming that Perry approached her while she was resting and engaged in non-consensual physical contact. The actor alleged that she immediately vomited following the incident and kept the matter secret for years. Separately stating Perry later helped assist with her U.S. visa process. Rose further stated that the incident was witnessed by others and that she possesses photographic evidence to support her claims.⁠
⁠
The timing of these public statements follows Rose’s long-standing criticism of Perry, including a 2017 dispute regarding Perry’s music and professional conduct. Reports state, Rose recently indicated that she has officially taken the matter to authorities, claiming in a social media post that she had just left a police station. ⁠
⁠
As of the time of the report, Katy Perry's team is pushing back, calling these allegations "categorically false" and "dangerous reckless lies."

⁠
Rose provided specific details of the alleged assault, claiming that Perry approached her while she was resting and engaged in non-consensual physical contact. The actor alleged that she immediately vomited following the incident and kept the matter secret for years. Separately stating Perry later helped assist with her U.S. visa process. Rose further stated that the incident was witnessed by others and that she possesses photographic evidence to support her claims.⁠
⁠
The timing of these public statements follows Rose’s long-standing criticism of Perry, including a 2017 dispute regarding Perry’s music and professional conduct. Reports state, Rose recently indicated that she has officially taken the matter to authorities, claiming in a social media post that she had just left a police station. ⁠
⁠
As of the time of the report, Katy Perry's team is pushing back, calling these allegations "categorically false" and "dangerous reckless lies."

During her headlining performance at Coachella 2026, Sabrina Carpenter reportedly faced criticism for her onstage reaction to a "Zaghrouta," a traditional Middle Eastern and North African vocal trill used to express joy. ⁠
⁠
While seated at her piano, Carpenter appeared confused by the high-pitched sound, labeling it "weird" and jokingly asking if it was a "yodel" or related to Burning Man. Her comments sparked immediate backlash online, with some social media users accusing the pop star of being insensitive and dismissive toward a cultural expression of celebration.⁠
⁠
In response to the controversy, Carpenter issued an apology on Saturday via social media, explaining that her reaction was rooted in "pure confusion" rather than ill intent. She noted that she could not see the specific crowd member or hear the sound clearly from the stage, leading to her sarcastic remarks. ⁠
⁠
Acknowledging that she "could have handled it better," the singer expressed her newfound understanding of what a Zaghrouta is and stated that she now welcomes all forms of cheers and celebratory chants from her audience.⁠
.⁠

Jasveen Sangha, the North Hollywood woman known as the “Ketamine Queen,” has been sentenced to 15 years in federal prison for her role in the death of actor Matthew Perry.

Sangha pleaded guilty to multiple charges, admitting to running a high-volume drug trafficking operation out of her home and supplying the ketamine that led to Perry’s fatal overdose in 2023.

During the sentencing, U.S. District Judge Sherilyn Peace Garnett reporedtedly identified Sangha as a primary figure in the conspiracy, noting she was "probably one of the most culpable" among the five defendants charged.

Reports state Sangha covered her mouth as she was handed her sentence, blowing a kiss to her family in the gallery as she left.

# Social Media Trends This Week

April 29, 2026

[Alex Oesterle](https://bluebearcreative.co/author/alex/)

![Social Media Trends This Week feature image: podium with gold star trend rising above in the center](https://bluebearcreative.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/10/social-media-trends-this-week-2025.webp)

How We Find Social Media Trends

Finding a reliable source for the latest social media trends had always been a pain point. So we decided to create that resource.

We used to have 1-2 people dedicated to endless hours of scrolling TikTok and Instagram Reels (ain’t nobody got time for that). But, with how individualized everyone’s feed has become, how can you be sure you’re getting exposure to the right trends at the right time with only a few perspectives?

That gave us an idea.

We decided to divvy up the responsibility of trend discovery, involving our entire team – the thinking was, the broader the range of interests in the mix, the broader the range of content coming up on social feeds. The result? More exposure to more trends and a better chance of identifying themes in the earlier stages of a trend’s life cycle.

Every week, our team compiles a list of all the top social media trends they’ve come across – from the emerging, newborn baby ones to the trends that have already gone full mainstream. From there, our strategists narrow in on the five best social media trends this week, neatly packaging them up for you here.

#### TREND **🔥** Heat Levels

|     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 🔥🔥🔥🔥 | 🔥🔥🔥 | 🔥🔥 | 🔥 |
| **HOT HOT HOT:**<br>Trend is mainstream. Act soon or miss out. | **Heating Up:**<br>Not yet at it’s peak temp; Brands are on it, but still time. | **Beginning to catch on:**<br>Other brands are on it, but it’s not wide-spread yet. | **Early, but worth watching:**<br>May or may not take off. |

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You set up a group for a big, dramatic jump on three. But when the countdown hits, only one person, usually the clueless one in the middle, actually jumps. The camera zooms in, and suddenly, there’s an announcement. Think: surprise prom dates, but with more suspense and less glitter.

**How to Capitalize:** Use this trend’s low-budget charm to announce a sale, menu drop, or product launch. Gather your team, cue the fake-out, and let one person ‘jump’ into the spotlight with your big news. It’s quick, playful, and feels like an inside joke your audience gets to share.

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** Do You Want To Go…

> TikTok Embed
>

**How to Capitalize:** Show off your most over-the-top product or restaurant experience with cinematic b-roll and the trending sound. The joke? Why rough it when your brand offers something way more extra. It’s a humblebrag, but with better lighting.

> [original sound - val wong⭐️](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7630260874699262723?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You’ve probably seen this: a soft baby yellow font pops up with ‘wait this looks so cool i have to capture it,’ then – bam – a montage of gorgeous footage or photography. It’s a simple, almost childlike hook that sets up a visual flex, and it’s catching on with creators who want to show off their best shots.

**How to Capitalize:** Showcase your product in its best light, literally. Use the yellow-font intro, then roll out a montage of stunning product shots, behind-the-scenes moments, or even a rapid-fire recipe compilation. It’s a scroll-stopper that feels authentic, not forced.

> [original sound - emomarcus96](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7589567274449783565?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You’ve probably heard that saxophone sound on TikTok, the one that gets louder as the situation gets more chaotic. Brands and creators are using it to capture the feeling of spiraling stress, usually with a comedic twist. It’s not brand new, but it’s still got plenty of life (and volume) left in it.

**How to Capitalize:** Picture this: your customer is staring at your menu, paralyzed by indecision, while the line behind them grows. That’s your cue to use the saxophone audio. It’s a relatable, funny way to highlight choice overload, and maybe nudge folks toward your bestsellers.

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** Fit Inspo

[![](<Base64-Image-Removed>)](https://www.tiktok.com/@aubreyscharpf/photo/7624630857164213517?is_from_webapp=1&sender_device=pc)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You know those childhood photos where your fashion sense peaked at age six? Creators are dusting them off, posting the wildest outfits, and labeling them ‘fit inspo.’ It’s nostalgia, humor, and a little self-roast. Basically, the internet’s favorite cocktail.

**How to Capitalize:** Dig up an old photo of your product, or someone holding it in the glory days, and slap ‘inspo’ on it. Or just join the fun with throwback outfits from your team. Either way, you get to show off your brand’s human side and score some relatability points.

* * *

**Trend Description:** World Stop is all about those blink-and-you-miss-it transformation edits. You freeze the action, then – bam – something changes. It’s a quick, visual way to spotlight before-and-after moments, and it’s picking up steam without feeling overplayed yet.

**How to Capitalize:** Show off your food in action: freeze the scene, then reveal a bite taken or a dish transformed. It’s a slick way to highlight product appeal and keep your audience glued to every frame.

**How to Capitalize:** Slip your product into the lineup of mystery items and let the guessing begin. Whether it’s a new drink, sauce, or snack, your brand gets a starring role in a game that’s equal parts chaos and taste test, perfect for playful, high-engagement content.

> [original sound - naddy🩹 - Soriko Philippines](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-naddy%F0%9F%A9%B9-7421283286535686929?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

**Trend Description:** This trend is all about the smug reveal. Someone says, ‘I heard your wife is really funny,’ and the camera cuts to the husband, who points out, ‘But you’re my wife.’ Cue the original speaker looking extra pleased with themselves. It’s a playful, self-aware format that’s making the rounds, just enough times that you know it’s hot, but not overcooked.

**How to Capitalize:** Swap in your product or brand for the ‘wife’ punchline. Think: ‘I heard your dogs love Waggin Train,’ with a cut to the dog owner, then back to the dog looking smug. Or, ‘I heard your partner is obsessed with Noodles,’ and let the pasta do the talking. It’s a clever way to spotlight brand loyalty with a wink.

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** Don’t Swipe

![](<Base64-Image-Removed>)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** The ‘Don’t Swipe’ trend is basically reverse psychology for your feed. You tell people not to swipe through your carousel, which of course makes them do exactly that. The payoff? A punchy reveal or message at the end. It’s simple, a little cheeky, and keeps people glued to your content.

**How to Capitalize:** Showcase your products in each carousel slide, building curiosity with every ‘don’t swipe’ prompt. Cap it off with a promo, a clever CTA, or just a nudge like ‘this is your sign to restock.’ It’s a playful way to boost engagement and sneak in your brand message.

* * *

> [EVERYTHING HALLELUJAH - Justin Bieber](https://www.tiktok.com/music/EVERYTHING-HALLELUJAH-7546504289062160400?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You’ve probably seen creators listing their favorite things over b-roll, punctuated by the word ‘Hallelujah’, all set to Justin Bieber’s ‘Everything Hallelujah.’ It’s a feel-good, rhythmic trend that’s all about celebrating the little (or big) joys, one hallelujah at a time. At this stage, it’s everywhere, but still has enough momentum to make your brand look in-the-know rather than late to the party.

**How to Capitalize:** Showcase your product’s perks or customer-loved features, each followed by a dramatic ‘Hallelujah.’ Or, riff on the original lyrics to highlight your brand’s versatility, think your product on a walk, in the sun, or with a lipstick mark. It’s a playful way to spotlight what makes you awesome, with a soundtrack that practically begs for engagement.

> [original sound - ℬ](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7608527302834146056?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You take basic b-roll, slap on text that says ‘My top 5 horror movies,’ and then list five things you secretly (or not-so-secretly) hate. The internet is running wild with this. Think humor, brutal honesty, and a dash of Katy Perry’s ‘The One That Got Away’ for dramatic flair. It’s a trend that’s all about the punchline, not the production value.

**How to Capitalize:** Your brand gets to play the relatable card by listing food or service ‘horrors’ like bland meals, missing ingredients, or those substitutions nobody asked for. Keep the visuals simple; the real magic is in the list. If it feels like a fan made it, you’re doing it right.

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

**Trend Description:** The AirPod Switch trend is all about creators swapping AirPods to instantly switch up the vibe, style, or mood of their group. It’s a quick, visual way to show off different personalities or aesthetics. Think of it as a TikTok wardrobe change, but for energy.

**How to Capitalize:** Showcase your brand’s versatility by ‘switching’ between product lines, menu items, or brand personas in a single video. It’s a playful way to highlight variety and keep your content feeling fresh, without needing a costume change.

> [original sound - The RAM Fam](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7625798283104963342?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 1 out of 4

**Trend Description:** Here’s a trend that’s as literal as it sounds: people drop random objects on their feet while holding a harmonica in their mouths, just to capture the accidental soundtrack. It’s slapstick, it’s musical, and it’s picking up steam with the ‘why not?’ crowd.

**How to Capitalize:** Hand your product to a creator, let gravity do its thing, and see what kind of harmonica chaos ensues. It’s a playful way to get your brand into the mix. Bonus points if your product makes a surprisingly melodic thud.

**🔥 Heat Level:** 4 out of 4

**Trend Description:** If Coachella content hasn’t hijacked your feed, you’re either a digital minimalist or living under a WiFi-proof rock. The festival is basically the influencer Olympics, and brands are everywhere, sometimes sincerely, sometimes with a wink.

**How to Capitalize:** This year, the real show is the influencer swarm. Brands are leaning in with everything from tongue-in-cheek fake activations to live-tweeting the festival chaos. If you want relevance, join the conversation whether you’re poking fun or playing along.

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** Loved You Then and I Love You Now

[![](<Base64-Image-Removed>)](https://www.tiktok.com/@savannahcampbell.9/photo/7624691756419992852?is_from_webapp=1&sender_device=pc)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** This trend is basically a nostalgia sandwich with a side of sentimentality. You use a carousel set to ‘Tongue Tied’ showing first, a shot of you with the lyric ‘take me to your best friend’s house.’ Next, an old photo with ‘i loved you then.’ Finally, a current photo with ‘i love you now.’ It’s a before-and-after, but with more feelings and less home renovation.

**How to Capitalize:** Swap out the personal photos for your brand’s glow-up moments. The ‘i loved you then’ slide? Cue a throwback to your vintage packaging or a pre-renovation storefront. The ‘i love you now’ slide? Show off your current look. It’s a low-effort way to flex your evolution and remind everyone you’ve still got it.

* * *

> [original sound - It’s Just Emma 🙂‍↔️](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7624204814443957023?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

**Trend Description:** Trying to explain the Summer House drama is like summarizing War and Peace in a tweet, just trust that ‘Carl’s a mess’ is the internet’s new shorthand for chaos. The phrase has become a meme-worthy catch-all for any situation that’s gone off the rails.

**How to Capitalize:** UberEats already jumped in, roping in cast members for extra flair. Your brand can riff on ‘Carl’s a mess’ to poke fun at everyday fails, product mishaps, or even menu chaos, bonus points if you can get a cameo from someone who’s actually survived a group chat meltdown.

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** “Involve Me”

[![](<Base64-Image-Removed>)](https://www.tiktok.com/@carsxnvasallx/photo/7619544343577234702?is_from_webapp=1&sender_device=pc)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You know that feeling when food looks so good you need a private moment? TikTok’s ‘Involve Me’ trend is all about that. Users post drool-worthy food pics, and the comments section turns into a confessional booth, think ‘involve me’ or ‘we can’t talk here’ as code for ‘I need this, now.’ It’s playful, a little secretive, and everyone’s in on the joke.

**How to Capitalize:** Post an unapologetically indulgent shot of your most irresistible menu item or product, think big, bold, and borderline excessive. Then, just sit back and watch as your comments fill up with fans begging to be part of the (not-so) secret club.

* * *

> [got 2 be real - sapphire](https://www.tiktok.com/music/got-2-be-real-6861537466566871814?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You’ve seen those viral memes, now creators are challenging friends and family to mimic the exact facial expressions. It’s a playful, low-lift trend that’s all about capturing those iconic, over-the-top reactions in real life. The result? Relatable, shareable content that feels like an inside joke with the internet.

**How to Capitalize:** Get your team in on the fun by recreating meme faces with your staff. It’s a chance to show off your brand’s personality, generate employee-generated content, and sneak in some subtle product placement, all while riding a trend that’s still got plenty of mileage left.

> [Loving Life Again - Ella Langley](https://www.tiktok.com/music/Loving-Life-Again-7619614676988807185?referer_url=bluebearcreative.co%2Fblog%2Fsocial-media-trends-this-week%2F&refer=embed&embed_source=121374463%2C121468991%2C121439635%2C121749182%2C121433650%2C121404359%2C121497414%2C122221973%2C122122240%2C121351166%2C121811500%2C121960941%2C122122244%2C122122243%2C122122242%2C121487028%2C121679410%2C122258714%2C121331973%2C120811592%2C120810756%2C121885509%3Bnull%3Bembed_song_name)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You know that wholesome audio making the rounds? Creators are pairing it with b-roll of the little things that make them fall for life all over again. It’s a feel-good scroll break, and yes, it’s everywhere, because apparently, we all need a reminder that joy exists.

**How to Capitalize:** Showcase your product or service as the star of someone’s ‘back to loving life’ moment. Pair it with the trending audio and a clever in-context twist (ICT), and suddenly your brand is the reason people are smiling at their screens.

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** Roommate Confrontations is that trend where creators hype up a dramatic showdown with their roommate, think ominous captions and suspenseful music, only for the ‘incident’ to be something hilariously mundane, like borrowing a sock or moving a mug.

**How to Capitalize:** Your brand can join the fun by staging a ‘tense’ moment over something trivial, like asking for an extra sauce packet or the last fry. It’s a low-lift, high-relatability way to sneak your product into the spotlight and show you get the internet’s sense of humor.

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** You’ve probably seen this: creators hold up empty hands, looking expectant, and when the beat drops, voilà, a product magically appears. It’s a visual punchline that’s simple, satisfying, and tailor-made for short-form video. The trend’s not brand new, but it’s still got plenty of juice left.

**How to Capitalize:** Hand your product the spotlight, literally. Film someone holding out their hand, then sync the reveal with a beat drop as your product pops into view. It’s low-effort, high-impact, and works for everything from burgers to shampoo bottles.

#### **Social Media Trend:** Tiny Workers

#### **Social Media Trend:** Priorities list

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

Someone posts their priorities, then a friend suggests something random (like grabbing your product), and suddenly that jumps to the top of the list. **How to Capitalize:** Drop your product or experience into the mix as the new top priority. Show how your brand is the plot twist that bumps everything else down the list. It’s a simple, relatable format that lets you join the conversation without reinventing the wheel, or the list.

#### **Social Media Trend:** Carousel Video Trend

[![](<Base64-Image-Removed>)](https://www.instagram.com/p/DVWECKWCH7s/?utm_source=ig_web_copy_link&igsh=NTc4MTIwNjQ2YQ==)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** Carousel Video is having a moment. Each slide pairs a video with a static image, split-screen style, so you can show off two sides of the same story. Think action and detail, demo and product shot, or process and result. It’s a format that keeps viewers swiping and your content feeling fresh, even if the trend isn’t brand new.

**How to Capitalize:** Break down a recipe, tutorial, or product demo by pairing each step’s video with a static shot of the ingredients, tools, or finished product. It’s a clever way to make complex info snackable, and your audience gets the full picture, literally.

#### **Social Media Trend:** Watch how my face changes WHEN I CUT OUT…

[![](<Base64-Image-Removed>)](https://www.instagram.com/reel/DVrPEIpDnXE/?utm_source=ig_web_copy_link&igsh=NTc4MTIwNjQ2YQ==)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 4

**Trend Description:** This trend plays with expectations by teasing a dramatic transformation. With text that says, ‘Watch how my face changes when I cut out…’ only to reveal the ‘sacrifice’ is actually mouthwatering food, and the punchline is a hilariously devastated face. It’s a bait-and-switch that’s relatable, a little bit petty, and very shareable. At a 3 out of 4 on the trend lifecycle, it’s still got some juice left for brands looking to jump in before it’s overdone.

**How to Capitalize:** Swap in your product for the food. Start with a hopeful face and the setup text, then show off your product in all its glory, and finish with the same face looking like it just lost its best friend. It’s quick, low-effort, and perfect for showing how unthinkable life would be without your brand, no Oscar-worthy acting required.

### 1/28/2026: SOCIAL MEDIA TRENDS THIS WEEK

#### **Social Media Trend:** Snow Ice Cream

> [@workeatplaylove](https://www.tiktok.com/@workeatplaylove?refer=embed "@workeatplaylove")
>
> There’s something about a snow day that makes you want to get outside and make core memories with your kids. So when I saw this idea (thanks arladk) I had to try it with my girls. To make your own ice cream: In a bowl, whisk: 1 1/2 cups cold heavy cream (I used 35%) with 1/3 cup powdered (icing) sugar and a splash of vanilla Make a little “nest” in clean snow the size of your bowl. Add a generous amount of salt to the hole (helps it freeze faster) and put your bowl in. Pack snow around it. Now the fun part. Take turns mixing (you can take breaks), until it thickens and becomes like soft serve ice cream (about 20 minutes). Don’t forget to include toppings. We used crushed Oreos. Serve and enjoy immediately. [#homemadeicecream](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/homemadeicecream?refer=embed "homemadeicecream") [#winteractivities](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/winteractivities?refer=embed "winteractivities") [#snowday](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/snowday?refer=embed "snowday") [#diyicecream](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/diyicecream?refer=embed "diyicecream") [#winter](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/winter?refer=embed "winter")

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** Snow ice cream is having a moment, again. You take heavy cream, sugar, vanilla, salt, and a generous scoop of actual snow, then mix in whatever your heart (or pantry) desires. It’s a nostalgia-fueled, DIY treat that turns snow days into content gold.

#### **Social Media Trend:** Lost control of my car

> [@bryannahernand3z](https://www.tiktok.com/@bryannahernand3z?refer=embed "@bryannahernand3z")
>
> fuhhhhh
>
>  [♬ original sound – Parker Coffaro](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7588308135597591309?refer=embed "♬ original sound - Parker Coffaro")

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** This trend is all about dash cam or phone footage paired with the deadpan caption, ‘lost control of my car today,’ as someone ‘accidentally’ ends up at a restaurant or drive-thru. It’s a tongue-in-cheek way to show irresistible cravings, no actual fender benders required.

**How to Capitalize:** Film your own version: have someone ‘lose control’ and wind up at your restaurant, drive-thru, or store. You can even take it further, show the journey from parking lot to product aisle, all under the guise of a snack-fueled detour.

**Trend Description:** You know the one: someone’s using the green screen effect to comment on a video behind them. #### **Social Media Trend:** Ins/Outs

[![](<Base64-Image-Removed>)](https://www.instagram.com/p/DTBZ40RgdjH/)

**🔥 Heat Level:** 4 out of 4

**Trend Description:** It’s that time of year when everyone’s making ‘Ins & Outs’ lists: What’s hot, what’s not, and what’s getting left behind in the group chat. Brands and creators are posting their takes, and audiences are chiming in with opinions, debates, and the occasional existential crisis over oat milk.

**How to Capitalize:** Slide your brand onto the ‘Ins’ list with a wink, or align your products with what your consumers want to see more of. Feeling bold? Toss in a playful jab at a competitor on the ‘Outs’ side. It’s a chance to show you’re in on the conversation, and maybe even start a few.

It’s a fresh, meme-able way to spotlight anticipation—think of it as the digital equivalent of stretching before doing literally anything.

**How to Capitalize:** Picture your brand’s mascot or team member stretching in front of a feast, with the caption ‘Warming up to absolutely demolish this plate of tacos.’ It’s a playful, low-lift way to show off your products and tap into the collective love of hyping up even the smallest moments.

**How to Capitalize:** Picture this: your brand’s signature product front and center, starring in a meal so photogenic it could model for Bon Appétit. Cast someone proudly presenting their dish, while a colleague or chef stands behind them giving the kind of approving/skeptical glare only true culinary gatekeepers can muster. Voilà—a hilarious, relatable way to spotlight your product and, bonus points, join the zeitgeist without looking like you’re trying too hard.

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** Bacon Avocado

> [@sophia.copp.spamm](https://www.tiktok.com/@sophia.copp.spamm?refer=embed "@sophia.copp.spamm")
>
> guys did i say bacon avocado quick enough?? \|\| [#fyp](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/fyp?refer=embed "fyp") [#fypシ](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/fyp%E3%82%B7?refer=embed "fypシ") [#baconavocado](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/baconavocado?refer=embed "baconavocado") [#bacon](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/bacon?refer=embed "bacon") [#avocado](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/avocado?refer=embed "avocado") [#trending](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/trending?refer=embed "trending") [#viral](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/viral?refer=embed "viral") [#viralvideo](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/viralvideo?refer=embed "viralvideo") [#fypageシ](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/fypage%E3%82%B7?refer=embed "fypageシ")
>
>  [♬ original sound – sophia copp spammy 🥳🥳](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7522712727056550687?refer=embed "♬ original sound - sophia copp spammy 🥳🥳")

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** Because clearly ‘bacon avocado’ wasn’t weird enough already, creators are now racing to say it at warp speed. Then, plot twist: instead of actually slowing it down, they cut to themselves unleashing a spicy, possibly unpopular opinion straight into the camera. Why use slow-mo when you can use suspense and existential dread?

**How to Capitalize:** Perfect for brands ready to stir the pot without actually starting a food fight. Picture this: your spokesperson does the ‘bacon avocado’ speed challenge, then—bam—smash cuts to their hottest, most deliciously divisive take about your product. Is pineapple on pizza a beverage crime? You decide. Bonus points if you split the internet.

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** My Name is Pink and I’m Really Glad to Meet You

> [@larabzzzzz](https://www.tiktok.com/@larabzzzzz?refer=embed "@larabzzzzz")
>
> Let’s see how it goes [#siblingcheck](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/siblingcheck?refer=embed "siblingcheck") [#married](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/married?refer=embed "married") [#fyp](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/fyp?refer=embed "fyp") @Ela @Nelly @lou
>
>  [♬ Illegal – PinkPantheress](https://www.tiktok.com/music/Illegal-7502057134566525713?refer=embed "♬ Illegal - PinkPantheress")

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** Because the internet needed more quirky meet-cutes, TikTokers are spinning the wheel of fate with ‘Illegal’ by PinkPantheress. The trend? Dramatic, sometimes hilariously awkward first encounters—think less ‘soulmate,’ more ‘stranger on a bus you’ll never see again.’ It’s all set to a soundtrack that’s just mysterious enough to make bumping into someone over spilled coffee seem like destiny.

**How to Capitalize:** Give your product some stars-in-its-eyes energy—cast it as the charismatic new acquaintance in this trend’s cinematic universe. Right when the lyrics drop, cue a cameo by your snack or sip, complete with the humblebrag ‘you were recommended to me by some people.’ Or, if you’re feeling spicy, turn up the surprise with an odd-couple pairing—like the dramatic introduction of Dr. Pepper and Grillo’s Pickles. It’s your chance to be the plot twist.

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** My Dream Date

> [@julia\_noelle](https://www.tiktok.com/@julia_noelle?refer=embed "@julia_noelle")
>
> my favorite hobby probably ever
>
>  [♬ original sound – Glens](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7516735042413562638?refer=embed "♬ original sound - Glens")

**🔥 Heat Level:** 3 out of 3

**Trend Description:** Meet “My Dream Date”—the trend where you hijack a Love Island audio to describe your ultimate date, but with a twist: you’re actually just reacting to someone’s latest move. It’s witty, it’s meta, and it’s got more layers than your last campaign brief. Your brand can jump in by playfully describing your product or service as the “dream date” in response to a customer’s action or review. It’s the perfect way to flex your personality, charm your audience, and show you’re fluent in meme. So, ready to make your brand the main character in the “My Dream Date” saga? Your followers are waiting.

**How to Capitalize:** Adding Lorem Ipsum so the automation doesn’t break

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** My Boyfriend Wants To Show You…

> [@yearningyardies](https://www.tiktok.com/@yearningyardies?refer=embed "@yearningyardies")
>
> isn’t he cool guys? 😤👊🏾 [#couple](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/couple?refer=embed "couple") [#boyfriend](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/boyfriend?refer=embed "boyfriend") [#plantdad](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/plantdad?refer=embed "plantdad") [#plantsoftiktok](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/plantsoftiktok?refer=embed "plantsoftiktok") [#relationship](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/relationship?refer=embed "relationship")
>
>  [♬ original sound – yearningyardies](https://www.tiktok.com/music/original-sound-7515039289009343262?refer=embed "♬ original sound - yearningyardies")

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 3

**Trend Description:** Hop on the “My Boyfriend Wants To Show You…” TikTok trend, where your brand can showcase new creations while someone stands by, adding a side of suspenseful support. Perfect for serving product buzz with a playful, slightly intimidating twist.

**How to Capitalize:** Jump on this viral moment by playfully revealing a dish your product “made,” using the My Boyfriend Wants To Show You… trend. Show off your creation—bonus points for a little over-the-top pride. It’s a clever, comic way to highlight your product in action and keep your brand part of the conversation (and laughs).

* * *

#### **Social Media Trend:** Ai Glass Cutting

> [@asmr.iatok](https://www.tiktok.com/@asmr.iatok?refer=embed "@asmr.iatok")
>
> ASMR glass cutting of multiple glass vegetables. 🔪✨ Crisp slices, clean sound — the most satisfying glass-fruit-slice ever. 🎧 [#glasscutting](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/glasscutting?refer=embed "glasscutting") [#glassfruit](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/glassfruit?refer=embed "glassfruit") [#slice](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/slice?refer=embed "slice") [#asmrglasscutting](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/asmrglasscutting?refer=embed "asmrglasscutting") [#asmrsound](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/asmrsound?refer=embed "asmrsound") [#satisfying](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/satisfying?refer=embed "satisfying") [#fyp](https://www.tiktok.com/tag/fyp?refer=embed "fyp")
>
>  [♬ som original – Asmr.ia](https://www.tiktok.com/music/som-original-7517680457622784824?refer=embed "♬ som original - Asmr.ia")

**🔥 Heat Level:** 2 out of 4

**Trend Description:** AI Glass Cutting is the lovechild of hyper-realistic AI visuals and the internet’s obsession with oddly satisfying ASMR. You get digital glass versions of everyday products, sliced up in a way that’s both mesmerizing and just a little bit confusing—for all the right reasons.

**How to Capitalize:** Reimagine your product as a glass sculpture, then ‘slice’ it in a video. The result? Scroll-stopping content that’s equal parts surreal and satisfying, with zero risk of actual glass in your DMs.
